				var = budget
				value = num_of_available_civilian_factories
			}
			#Research slots cost

				var = cost_of_research_slots
				value = amount_research_slots
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				var = cost_of_research_slots
				value = 25
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = budget
				value = cost_of_research_slots
